# OEMNVBK sample reverse-engineering report

Pure binary analysis of all samples under `resources/`. Generated by `scripts/re_analyze_samples.py`.

## Executive summary

All five samples share one **unified TLV record stream** per sub-file. With the corrected descriptor layout (`record_count` as **u32 LE** at bytes 0–3), walked record counts match the descriptor **exactly** and payload coverage is **100%** (records + trailing sector zero-pad) on every non-truncated sub-file.

### Coverage summary

| Sample | Flag | Subs | SHA OK | Rec match | Avg cov% | Min cov% | PATH | ID | Ext 0xF* | Go path-only fraction |
|---|---:|---:|---:|---:|---:|---:|---:|---:|---:|---|
| `oem_stanvbk-2019-10-23` | 0x00 | 7 | 7/7 | 7/7 | 100.0 | 100.0 | 4865 | 1693 | 0 | 4865/6558 |
| `op7t_oem_stanvbk.img` | 0x00 | 6 | 6/6 | 6/6 | 100.0 | 100.0 | 110 | 147 | 10 | 110/267 |
| `op8pro_o2os_10.5.6.in11ba_dycnvbk_trimmed.img` | 0x01 | 1 | 0/1 | 1/1 | 100.0 | 100.0 | 7 | 23 | 16 | 1/33 |
| `op8pro_o2os_10.5.6.in11ba_stanvbk_trimmed.img` | 0x01 | 10 | 9/10 | 10/10 | 100.0 | 100.0 | 200 | 333 | 19 | 200/552 |
| `oplusstanvbk.img` | 0x02 | 12 | 12/12 | 12/12 | 100.0 | 100.0 | 181 | 319 | 18 | 181/518 |

> **Go path-only fraction:** records with `kind==0x02` that current `parseEntries` can see (it still misses leading/interleaved ID items and stops on non-0x0001 markers).

## Corrected binary layouts

### Header (sector 0, 0x200 bytes)

```
offset  size   field
0x00    8      magic "OEMNVBK\0"
0x08    4      version  (STA: 01 00 01 01; DYC: 01 00 01 00)
0x0c    u8     sub_file_count
0x0d    u32le  table_offset  (always 0x1c in samples)
0x11    u8     header_flag   (0x00 older, 0x01 OP8-era, 0x02 newer oplus)
0x12    3      build_time    YY MM DD binary (not BCD)
0x15    u8     reserved      (0x00 all samples)
0x16    6      signature_or_reserved  (zeros, except oplus ASCII-ish)
0x1c    0x29*N descriptor table (may spill past 0x200 when N large)
```

### Descriptor (0x29 = 41 bytes each)

```
offset  size   field
0x00    u32le  record_count     *** NOT u8 + 3 unknown ***
0x04    u16le  start_sector     payload_off = start_sector * 512
0x06    u16le  num_sectors      payload_len = num_sectors * 512
0x08    32     sha256           of full payload including zero pad
0x28    u8     rf_id            0xff = common/manifest; else RF variant
```

**Correction vs current Go parser:** `CountHint byte` + ignored `unk[1:3]` is wrong. Those four bytes are a single little-endian record count. On 2019 RF sub-files this is `0x000004ad = 1197`, which was previously misread as hint=`0xad` + unk=`04 00 00`.

### Payload record stream (100% of non-pad bytes)

Each sub-file payload is:

```
record[record_count] ... trailing 0x00 pad to num_sectors*512
```

#### Common header (12 bytes)

```
offset  size   field
0x00    u32le  total            full record size including this header
0x04    u32le  tag              packed fields (see below)
0x08    u16le  field_a          meaning depends on kind
0x0a    u16le  field_b          meaning depends on kind
0x0c    …      payload          total-12 bytes
```

#### Tag packing (little-endian byte order)

```
tag bytes:  [kind] [sub] [rf] [cat]
  kind  u8  record kind / flags (low nibble primary type)
  sub   u8  subtype / attribute (0x09 common, also 0x0d, 0x19, 0x29, 0x39, 0x40…)
  rf    u8  matches sub-file RF ID (always in samples)
  cat   u8  category (0x10 RF/modem, 0x18 OEM/policy, 0x50/0x70 large/zlib-ish…)
```

Examples:

| Tag LE bytes | kind | sub | rf | cat | Meaning |
|---|---:|---:|---:|---:|---|
| `02 09 ff 10` → `0x10ff0902` | 0x02 | 0x09 | 0xff | 0x10 | path item, common RF |
| `01 09 0f 10` → `0x100f0901` | 0x01 | 0x09 | 0x0f | 0x10 | numeric NV, RF 0x0f |
| `01 09 7f 50` → `0x507f0901` | 0x01 | 0x09 | 0x7f | 0x50 | numeric, cat 0x50 (often zlib body) |
| `f3 09 7f 10` → `0x107f09f3` | 0xf3 | 0x09 | 0x7f | 0x10 | extended large ID item |

#### kind = 0x01 — numeric NV item

```
[u32 total][u32 tag][u16 nv_id][u16 dataLen][data…]
```

- `dataLen == total - 12 == len(data)` always for kind 0x01 in samples.
- `data` may be raw bytes, raw zlib (`78 9c…`), or `VTNV` wrapper + zlib.

#### kind = 0x02 — path / EFS item

```
[u32 total][u32 tag][u16 type=0x0001][u16 pathLen]
[path bytes, pathLen, typically NUL-terminated ASCII]
[u16 sep=0x0002][u16 dataLen][data…]
```

- Current Go `parseEntries` only understands this kind (and only after scanning).
- `dataLen` usually equals remaining bytes after the dataLen field.

#### kind = 0xF1 / 0xF2 / 0xF3 / 0xF4 — extended / large items

| Kind | Low nibble | Role | field_a | field_b | Notes |
|---:|---:|---|---|---|---|
| 0xF1 | 0x1 | large numeric | nv_id | often == data size | DYC-heavy; body often VTNV+zlib |
| 0xF2 | 0x2 | large path | 0x0001 | pathLen | path layout like 0x02; huge payloads |
| 0xF3 | 0x1 | large numeric | nv_id | often **≠** full size | short lead u16s then VTNV/zlib; multi-chunk feel |
| 0xF4 | 0x2 | large path | 0x0001 | pathLen | seen once on oplus manifest (huge path item) |

Outer framing still uses `total` for sizing, so the stream remains 100% walkable even when `field_b` is not a plain data length for 0xF3.

##### 0xF3 payload lead (observed)

```
u16 unk0;          // often 1 or small count
u16 size_or_attr;  // frequently equals field_b
u16 unk1;          // often 1
// then either:
//   zlib stream directly, or
//   VTNV wrapper:
//     char magic[4] = "VTNV";
//     u16 version;    // 0x0001
//     u16 field;      // size/count-ish
//     zlib…
```

##### VTNV + nested RFNV directory

Many large RF payloads decompress to blobs whose header matches the Go parser’s **ID directory** heuristic (`byte4==0x34`, count at offset 7, 24-byte groups of four `00 00 00 00 + u16 id` slots). That directory is a **nested** encoding inside compressed item data — **not** the top-level OEMNVBK container format.

```
decomp[0:16] header
  byte4 = 0x34
  byte7 = group_count
decomp[16:]  group_count * 24 bytes
  each group: 4 slots × (u32 zero + u16 id)
```

NV item chains (`u16 id` + `u16 total` + payload) also appear inside some decompressed blobs.

## DYCNVBK vs STANVBK

| Aspect | DYC (OP8 Pro) | STA (OP8 Pro) |
|---|---|---|
| File | `op8pro_o2os_10.5.6.in11ba_dycnvbk_trimmed.img` | `op8pro_o2os_10.5.6.in11ba_stanvbk_trimmed.img` |
| Version | `01000100` | `01000101` |
| HeaderFlag | 0x01 | 0x01 |
| Build | 2020-03-21 | 2020-04-26 |
| Sub-files | 1 (RF 0xff only) | 10 (0xff + many RF) |
| Kind mix | {'0x01': 16, '0x02': 1, '0xf1': 7, '0xf2': 6, '0xf3': 3} | {'0x01': 333, '0x02': 200, '0xf3': 19} |
| Extended kinds | F1/F2/F3 heavy | mostly 01/02 + some F3 |
| Trimmed | yes (SHA TRUNC) | last sub truncated |

### Structural observations

1. **Same container**: both are OEMNVBK header + descriptor table + per-sub TLV streams.
2. **DYC** = single dynamic/common partition (`rf=0xff`) holding device-unique-ish NV (IMEI-related IDs, certs, large F1/F3 blobs). Version nibble ends in `00`.
3. **STA** = multi-RF static calibration/config: sub0 is small common manifest (`rf=0xff`), subs 1..N are per-RF-card images with matching `tag.rf`.
4. **DYC uses extended kinds** (0xF1 path-sized numeric, 0xF2 large paths, 0xF3 huge items) far more than STA; STA RF subs are mostly kind 0x01/0x02 with occasional 0xF3.
5. Both may embed **VTNV+zlib** and nested RFNV ID directories inside large item payloads.

### Cross-sample header matrix

| Sample | Flag | Ver | Subs | Build | Sig[6] | Table end | First payload sector |
|---|---:|---|---:|---|---|---:|---:|
| `oem_stanvbk-2019-10-23` | 0x00 | 01000101 | 7 | 2019-10-08 | `000000000000` | 0x13b | 1 |
| `op7t_oem_stanvbk.img` | 0x00 | 01000101 | 6 | 2019-09-25 | `000000000000` | 0x112 | 1 |
| `op8pro_o2os_10.5.6.in11ba_dycnvbk_trimmed.img` | 0x01 | 01000100 | 1 | 2020-03-21 | `000000000000` | 0x45 | 1 |
| `op8pro_o2os_10.5.6.in11ba_stanvbk_trimmed.img` | 0x01 | 01000101 | 10 | 2020-04-26 | `000000000000` | 0x1b6 | 1 |
| `oplusstanvbk.img` | 0x02 | 01000101 | 12 | 2024-12-24 | `356132613431` | 0x208 | 2 |

Note: `oplusstanvbk.img` table ends at `0x208` (spills 8 bytes into sector 1); first payload starts at sector 2. Flag `0x02` and non-zero sig region `35 61 32 61 34 31` (`5a2a41`).

## Current Go parser vs full decode

| Area | Go (`pkg/nvbk_parser.go`) | Reality from RE |
|---|---|---|
| Descriptor count | `CountHint` u8 at byte 0; bytes 1–3 ignored | **u32 LE record_count** at bytes 0–3 |
| Payload model | Path scan **or** zlib NV directory | **Unified TLV stream** of PATH+ID+extended |
| Path entries | Scan for `type=0x0001` & `tag&0xff==0x02`; stop on other types | Contiguous stream; ID records use same header with kind=0x01 |
| ID records | Only via nested zlib directory + ID+total chain | First-class kind=0x01 records with `nv_id` at field_a |
| Extended kinds | Unknown / treated as stop or skip | 0xF1–0xF4 walkable via `total`; bodies often VTNV+zlib |
| Zlib search | `78 9c` only inside raw subfile | Also `78 01`/`78 da`; usually **inside** record payloads |
| Coverage | No accounting | 100% with TLV walk + zero pad |

### Top gaps blocking “full decode” in Go today

| Rank | Gap | Impact | Fix direction |
|---:|---|---|---|
| 1 | No contiguous TLV walker for kind 0x01 / 0xF* | Loses majority of records on RF subs & DYC | Implement `walkRecords` using `total` + tag.kind |
| 2 | `CountHint` u8 instead of u32 `record_count` | Wrong item counts when count > 255 | Read u32 at desc[0:4] |
| 3 | Path parser stops at non-0x0001 field_a | Drops trailing ID records after first non-path | Kind dispatch, not typeMarker-only |
| 4 | Extended kind body formats (F3 lead, VTNV) | Large RF blobs not semantically decoded | Parse VTNV + zlib; keep nested dir as secondary |
| 5 | Nested RFNV directory treated as primary format | Misleading model of “compressed subfiles” | Demote to payload codec inside ID items |
| 6 | Trimmed samples | Incomplete last payloads / SHA | Use full images for verification |

#### Sub[0] RF=0xff — mixed-records

- Descriptor: `4b00000001000d008c7ad3e680e1e3969207303a30abc78abb5d488337076409a5d541e9a7a6654cff`
- Payload @ 0x200, 6656 bytes (expect 6656), walk_end=0x1810, pad=496
- Prefix: `0d0000000109ff102e11010000110000000109ff10dc1a050000000000050e0000000109ff10fb1a0200010051000000`
- Coverage: **100.0%** (nonzero 100.0%)
- Nested NV directories in payloads: 0 (ids listed: 0)
- Go gap: Go misses 3 leading ID/extended records before first path
- Go gap: Go misses 21 ID/extended records interleaved/after paths (stops or skips)
- Go gap: Go path-entry path recovers ≤51/75 records (kind==0x02 only)

## Records that are NOT path type 0x0001 (Go skips/stops)

Under the unified model these are not “mystery typeMarkers” — they are **kind=0x01/0xF*** records where `field_a` is an NV item ID (or pathLen for F2/F4), not a type enum.

### Misread by old scanner

Old interpretation of ID record `13 00 00 00 01 09 ff 10 2e 11 01 00 00`:

```
total=13 tag=0x10ff0901 typeMarker=0x112e pathLen=1  → rejected (type≠1)
```

Correct interpretation:

```
total=13 tag=0x10ff0901 nv_id=0x112e dataLen=1 data=[0x00]
```

### Kind histogram (all samples)

| Kind | Count | Role |
|---|---:|---|
| 0x02 | 5357 | path/EFS item |
| 0x01 | 2508 | numeric NV item |
| 0xf3 | 49 | extended large numeric (lead hdr + VTNV/zlib) |
| 0xf1 | 7 | extended large numeric |
| 0xf2 | 6 | extended large path |
| 0xf4 | 1 | extended large path (oplus) |

### Tag `cat` / `sub` observations

| Field | Values seen | Notes |
|---|---|---|
| cat 0x10 | dominant on RF subs | modem/RF calibration class |
| cat 0x18 | common on manifests / OEM paths | policy, SUPL certs, OEM files |
| cat 0x50 / 0x70 | with kind 0x01 on RF | often zlib-compressed numeric payloads |
| sub 0x09 | most common | default attribute |
| sub 0x0d | RF items | often larger / F3 companions |
| sub 0x19 / 0x29 / 0x39 / 0x40 | variants | subscription / feature slices |

## Methodology

1. Parse header + descriptors; treat desc[0:4] as u32 record_count.
2. Slice payload by sector range; SHA-256 verify when not truncated.
3. Walk records by `total` until 12 zero bytes / EOF.
4. Dispatch on `tag.kind` low nibble (1=ID, 2=PATH) and high nibble (0xF=extended).
5. Classify payloads: raw / zlib / VTNV / nested RFNV directory.
6. Coverage = walk_end + trailing zero pad vs payload length.
7. Compare walked count to descriptor record_count.

## Artifacts

- Report: `docs/re-samples-decode.md`
- JSON dump: `scripts/re_analyze_samples.json`
- Script: `scripts/re_analyze_samples.py`
- Go parser (unchanged): `pkg/nvbk_parser.go`
